Mode</a></div></div></div><div class="hxfnim0 _1x6sixh2"><div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1ts"><article class="hxfnim0"><p data-algolia-lvl0="true" style="display:none">Migration Guide</p><h1 class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hd _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzozp fo5aobt _1g1ptzolo fo5aobm fo5aobp">Migration Guide</h1>
<h2 class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo10e _1g1ptzo1bs fo5aobt _1g1ptzol9 fo5aobj fo5aobq">Migrating RainbowKit</h2>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzozu _1g1ptzo1d6 _1g1ptzo2bo" id="2xx-breaking-changes"><a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="#2xx-breaking-changes"><h3 class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hd _1g1ptzoe1 _1g1ptzo2b6 fo5aobt _1g1ptzole fo5aobg fo5aobs">2.x.x Breaking changes</h3></a></div>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">The <a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="https://wagmi.sh">wagmi</a> and <a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="https://viem.sh">viem</a> peer dependencies have reached <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">2.x.x</code> with breaking changes.</p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">Follow the steps below to migrate.</p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px"><strong>1. Upgrade RainbowKit, <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">wagmi</code>, and <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">viem</code> to their latest versions</strong></p>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1cc _1g1ptzo109 _1g1ptzo46 _1g1ptzo1yu" style="overflow:hidden"><pre class="hxfnim0 o4oa330"><code><div data-line="1" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token function">npm</span> i @rainbow-me/rainbowkit@2 wagmi@2 <a href="/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection" class="__cf_email__" data-cfemail="f98f909c94b9cbd781">[email&#160;protected]</a>
</div></code></pre><div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1yk _1g1ptzo1zj _1g1ptzo23u" data-copy="true"><button class="hxfnim0 hxfnim9 _1ct8fpb1n _1g1ptzo5 _1g1ptzo2b4 _1g1ptzoe6 _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo2c0 _1g1ptzo2c2 _1g1ptzo3wu _1g1ptzo3x2 _1g1ptzo3x8 _1ct8fpb11 _1ct8fpb23 _1g1ptzo1ta _1g1ptzo1vd _1g1ptzol4 _1g1ptzomn _1ct8fpb7 _1g1ptzo3gd _1ct8fpbe _1g1ptzo230 _1g1ptzouf _1g1ptzo3w _1ct8fpb1m" tabindex="-1" style="background-color:var(--colors-lightBlue);box-shadow:0 0 8px var(--colors-fillElevated)"><svg fill="none" height="24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><title>Copy</title><path d="M3.875 19.727c0 1.687.867 2.562 2.54 2.562h7.312c1.671 0 2.53-.883 2.53-2.562V18.28h1.329c1.672 0 2.539-.875 2.539-2.562V9.53c0-1.023-.21-1.68-.828-2.312L15.398 3.25c-.585-.602-1.28-.828-2.18-.828h-2.945c-1.664 0-2.539.875-2.539 2.562v1.438h-1.32c-1.672 0-2.539.883-2.539 2.562v10.743Zm11.602-8.211L11.242 7.21c-.601-.61-1.11-.774-1.976-.781V5.07c0-.718.382-1.117 1.14-1.117h3.266v3.735c0 .968.515 1.468 1.476 1.468h3.446v6.469c0 .727-.375 1.125-1.14 1.125h-1.196v-3.031c0-1.055-.125-1.54-.781-2.203Zm-.524-4.024V4.586l3.242 3.289h-2.86c-.265 0-.382-.11-.382-.383Zm-9.547 12.14V9.079c0-.719.375-1.125 1.133-1.125h2.399v4.281c0 1.118.554 1.664 1.664 1.664h4.125v5.735c0 .726-.375 1.125-1.133 1.125H6.539c-.758 0-1.133-.399-1.133-1.125Zm5.344-7.085c-.32 0-.46-.14-.46-.461V8.25l4.226 4.297H10.75Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></button></div><div data-pre-gradient="true"></div></div>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px"><strong>2. Install <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">@tanstack/react-query</code> peer dependency</strong></p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">With Wagmi v2, <a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="https://tanstack.com/query/v5/docs/react/overview">TanStack Query</a> is now a required peer dependency.</p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">Install it with the following command:</p>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1cc _1g1ptzo109 _1g1ptzo46 _1g1ptzo1yu" style="overflow:hidden"><pre class="hxfnim0 o4oa330"><code><div data-line="1" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token function">npm</span> i @tanstack/react-query
</div></code></pre><div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1yk _1g1ptzo1zj _1g1ptzo23u" data-copy="true"><button class="hxfnim0 hxfnim9 _1ct8fpb1n _1g1ptzo5 _1g1ptzo2b4 _1g1ptzoe6 _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo2c0 _1g1ptzo2c2 _1g1ptzo3wu _1g1ptzo3x2 _1g1ptzo3x8 _1ct8fpb11 _1ct8fpb23 _1g1ptzo1ta _1g1ptzo1vd _1g1ptzol4 _1g1ptzomn _1ct8fpb7 _1g1ptzo3gd _1ct8fpbe _1g1ptzo230 _1g1ptzouf _1g1ptzo3w _1ct8fpb1m" tabindex="-1" style="background-color:var(--colors-lightBlue);box-shadow:0 0 8px var(--colors-fillElevated)"><svg fill="none" height="24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><title>Copy</title><path d="M3.875 19.727c0 1.687.867 2.562 2.54 2.562h7.312c1.671 0 2.53-.883 2.53-2.562V18.28h1.329c1.672 0 2.539-.875 2.539-2.562V9.53c0-1.023-.21-1.68-.828-2.312L15.398 3.25c-.585-.602-1.28-.828-2.18-.828h-2.945c-1.664 0-2.539.875-2.539 2.562v1.438h-1.32c-1.672 0-2.539.883-2.539 2.562v10.743Zm11.602-8.211L11.242 7.21c-.601-.61-1.11-.774-1.976-.781V5.07c0-.718.382-1.117 1.14-1.117h3.266v3.735c0 .968.515 1.468 1.476 1.468h3.446v6.469c0 .727-.375 1.125-1.14 1.125h-1.196v-3.031c0-1.055-.125-1.54-.781-2.203Zm-.524-4.024V4.586l3.242 3.289h-2.86c-.265 0-.382-.11-.382-.383Zm-9.547 12.14V9.079c0-.719.375-1.125 1.133-1.125h2.399v4.281c0 1.118.554 1.664 1.664 1.664h4.125v5.735c0 .726-.375 1.125-1.133 1.125H6.539c-.758 0-1.133-.399-1.133-1.125Zm5.344-7.085c-.32 0-.46-.14-.46-.461V8.25l4.226 4.297H10.75Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></button></div><div data-pre-gradient="true"></div></div>

<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px"><strong>4. Check for breaking changes in <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">wagmi</code> and <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">viem</code></strong></p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">If you use <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">wagmi</code> hooks and <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">viem</code> actions in your dApp, you will need to follow the migration guides for v2:</p>
<ul class="hxfnim0 hxfnim1 _1g1ptzo109 _1g1ptzo1sq">
<li class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo5 _1g1ptzodr"><span class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo2q1 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzoeb _1g1ptzoog _1g1ptzo186 _1g1ptzo27v"></span><div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px"><a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="https://wagmi.sh/react/guides/migrate-from-v1-to-v2">Wagmi v2 Migration Guide</a></div></li>
<li class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo5 _1g1ptzodr"><span class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo2q1 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzoeb _1g1ptzoog _1g1ptzo186 _1g1ptzo27v"></span><div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px"><a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="https://viem.sh/docs/migration-guide#2xx-breaking-changes">Viem v2 Breaking Changes</a></div></li>
</ul>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzozu _1g1ptzo1d1 _1g1ptzo2bo" id="rainbowkit-changes"><a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="#rainbowkit-changes"><h4 class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hd _1g1ptzoe1 _1g1ptzo2b6 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol9 fo5aobj fo5aobs">RainbowKit Changes</h4></a></div>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px"><strong>1. Improved behavior for EIP-6963 wallets</strong></p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">Wallets that support the new EIP-6963 connection standard (including Rainbow, MetaMask, and more) will now automatically appear in an <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">Installed</code> section during the Connect Wallet experience. This ensures that users can always find their favorite wallets and connect to dApps without conflicts or fallback buttons.</p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">Developers continue to have full control over the Custom Wallet List to emphasize preferred wallets for end users. It is encouraged that you continue to include the <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">injectedWallet</code> and <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">walletConnectWallet</code> in your list to supports all platforms.</p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px"><strong>2. Wagmi configuration with getDefaultConfig</strong></p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">This new API simplifies the configuration experience and replaces the need to use Wagmi&#x27;s <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">createConfig</code> directly. Chain configuration is simplified, including inferred public providers for <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">transports</code>.</p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">The default wallet list will be automatically included, deprecating the need to use <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">getDefaultWallets</code> and <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">connectorsForWallets</code>.</p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">You can create a Custom Wallet List by passing imported or Custom Wallet connectors to <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">wallets</code>. Instantiating wallet connectors and passing <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">projectId</code> and <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">chains</code> is no longer required.</p>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1cc _1g1ptzo109 _1g1ptzo46 _1g1ptzo1yu" style="overflow:hidden"><pre class="hxfnim0 o4oa330"><code><div data-line="1" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">const config = getDefaultConfig({
</div><div data-line="2" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  appName: &#x27;RainbowKit demo&#x27;,
</div><div data-line="3" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  projectId: &#x27;YOUR_PROJECT_ID&#x27;,
</div><div data-line="4" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  chains: [mainnet],
</div><div data-line="5" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  wallets: [rainbowWallet], /<span class="token italic"><span class="token punctuation">*</span><span class="token content"> optional custom wallet list </span><span class="token punctuation">*</span></span>/
</div><div data-line="6" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">  /<span class="token italic"><span class="token punctuation">*</span><span class="token content"> Wagmi createConfig options including <span class="token code-snippet code keyword">`transports`</span> are also accepted </span><span class="token punctuation">*</span></span>/
</div><div data-line="7" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">})
</div></code></pre><div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1yk _1g1ptzo1zj _1g1ptzo23u" data-copy="true"><button class="hxfnim0 hxfnim9 _1ct8fpb1n _1g1ptzo5 _1g1ptzo2b4 _1g1ptzoe6 _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo2c0 _1g1ptzo2c2 _1g1ptzo3wu _1g1ptzo3x2 _1g1ptzo3x8 _1ct8fpb11 _1ct8fpb23 _1g1ptzo1ta _1g1ptzo1vd _1g1ptzol4 _1g1ptzomn _1ct8fpb7 _1g1ptzo3gd _1ct8fpbe _1g1ptzo230 _1g1ptzouf _1g1ptzo3w _1ct8fpb1m" tabindex="-1" style="background-color:var(--colors-lightBlue);box-shadow:0 0 8px var(--colors-fillElevated)"><svg fill="none" height="24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><title>Copy</title><path d="M3.875 19.727c0 1.687.867 2.562 2.54 2.562h7.312c1.671 0 2.53-.883 2.53-2.562V18.28h1.329c1.672 0 2.539-.875 2.539-2.562V9.53c0-1.023-.21-1.68-.828-2.312L15.398 3.25c-.585-.602-1.28-.828-2.18-.828h-2.945c-1.664 0-2.539.875-2.539 2.562v1.438h-1.32c-1.672 0-2.539.883-2.539 2.562v10.743Zm11.602-8.211L11.242 7.21c-.601-.61-1.11-.774-1.976-.781V5.07c0-.718.382-1.117 1.14-1.117h3.266v3.735c0 .968.515 1.468 1.476 1.468h3.446v6.469c0 .727-.375 1.125-1.14 1.125h-1.196v-3.031c0-1.055-.125-1.54-.781-2.203Zm-.524-4.024V4.586l3.242 3.289h-2.86c-.265 0-.382-.11-.382-.383Zm-9.547 12.14V9.079c0-.719.375-1.125 1.133-1.125h2.399v4.281c0 1.118.554 1.664 1.664 1.664h4.125v5.735c0 .726-.375 1.125-1.133 1.125H6.539c-.758 0-1.133-.399-1.133-1.125Zm5.344-7.085c-.32 0-.46-.14-.46-.461V8.25l4.226 4.297H10.75Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></button></div><div data-pre-gradient="true"></div></div>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px"><strong>3. RainbowKitProvider</strong></p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">You no longer need to pass <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">chains</code> to <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">&lt;RainbowKitProvider&gt;</code>.</p>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1cc _1g1ptzo109 _1g1ptzo46 _1g1ptzo1yu" style="overflow:hidden"><pre class="hxfnim0 o4oa330"><code><div data-line="1" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token deleted-sign deleted"><span class="token prefix deleted">-</span><span class="token line"> &lt;RainbowKitProvider chains={chains}&gt;</span>
<span class="token line"></span></span><span class="token inserted-sign inserted"><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line"> &lt;RainbowKitProvider&gt;</span>
<span class="token line"></span></span></div></code></pre><div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1yk _1g1ptzo1zj _1g1ptzo23u" data-copy="true"><button class="hxfnim0 hxfnim9 _1ct8fpb1n _1g1ptzo5 _1g1ptzo2b4 _1g1ptzoe6 _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo2c0 _1g1ptzo2c2 _1g1ptzo3wu _1g1ptzo3x2 _1g1ptzo3x8 _1ct8fpb11 _1ct8fpb23 _1g1ptzo1ta _1g1ptzo1vd _1g1ptzol4 _1g1ptzomn _1ct8fpb7 _1g1ptzo3gd _1ct8fpbe _1g1ptzo230 _1g1ptzouf _1g1ptzo3w _1ct8fpb1m" tabindex="-1" style="background-color:var(--colors-lightBlue);box-shadow:0 0 8px var(--colors-fillElevated)"><svg fill="none" height="24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><title>Copy</title><path d="M3.875 19.727c0 1.687.867 2.562 2.54 2.562h7.312c1.671 0 2.53-.883 2.53-2.562V18.28h1.329c1.672 0 2.539-.875 2.539-2.562V9.53c0-1.023-.21-1.68-.828-2.312L15.398 3.25c-.585-.602-1.28-.828-2.18-.828h-2.945c-1.664 0-2.539.875-2.539 2.562v1.438h-1.32c-1.672 0-2.539.883-2.539 2.562v10.743Zm11.602-8.211L11.242 7.21c-.601-.61-1.11-.774-1.976-.781V5.07c0-.718.382-1.117 1.14-1.117h3.266v3.735c0 .968.515 1.468 1.476 1.468h3.446v6.469c0 .727-.375 1.125-1.14 1.125h-1.196v-3.031c0-1.055-.125-1.54-.781-2.203Zm-.524-4.024V4.586l3.242 3.289h-2.86c-.265 0-.382-.11-.382-.383Zm-9.547 12.14V9.079c0-.719.375-1.125 1.133-1.125h2.399v4.281c0 1.118.554 1.664 1.664 1.664h4.125v5.735c0 .726-.375 1.125-1.133 1.125H6.539c-.758 0-1.133-.399-1.133-1.125Zm5.344-7.085c-.32 0-.46-.14-.46-.461V8.25l4.226 4.297H10.75Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></button></div><div data-pre-gradient="true"></div></div>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px"><strong>4. Custom Chains</strong></p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">The <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">Chain</code> type has changed in accordance with Wagmi v2, and continues to support RainbowKit&#x27;s <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">iconUrl</code> and <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">iconBackground</code> metadata.</p>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1cc _1g1ptzo109 _1g1ptzo46 _1g1ptzo1yu" style="overflow:hidden"><pre class="hxfnim0 o4oa330"><code><div data-line="1" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token inserted-sign inserted"><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line"> import { Chain } from &#x27;@rainbow-me/rainbowkit&#x27;</span>
<span class="token line"></span></span>

<span class="token line"></span></span></div></code></pre><div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1yk _1g1ptzo1zj _1g1ptzo23u" data-copy="true"><button class="hxfnim0 hxfnim9 _1ct8fpb1n _1g1ptzo5 _1g1ptzo2b4 _1g1ptzoe6 _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo2c0 _1g1ptzo2c2 _1g1ptzo3wu _1g1ptzo3x2 _1g1ptzo3x8 _1ct8fpb11 _1ct8fpb23 _1g1ptzo1ta _1g1ptzo1vd _1g1ptzol4 _1g1ptzomn _1ct8fpb7 _1g1ptzo3gd _1ct8fpbe _1g1ptzo230 _1g1ptzouf _1g1ptzo3w _1ct8fpb1m" tabindex="-1" style="background-color:var(--colors-lightBlue);box-shadow:0 0 8px var(--colors-fillElevated)"><svg fill="none" height="24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><title>Copy</title><path d="M3.875 19.727c0 1.687.867 2.562 2.54 2.562h7.312c1.671 0 2.53-.883 2.53-2.562V18.28h1.329c1.672 0 2.539-.875 2.539-2.562V9.53c0-1.023-.21-1.68-.828-2.312L15.398 3.25c-.585-.602-1.28-.828-2.18-.828h-2.945c-1.664 0-2.539.875-2.539 2.562v1.438h-1.32c-1.672 0-2.539.883-2.539 2.562v10.743Zm11.602-8.211L11.242 7.21c-.601-.61-1.11-.774-1.976-.781V5.07c0-.718.382-1.117 1.14-1.117h3.266v3.735c0 .968.515 1.468 1.476 1.468h3.446v6.469c0 .727-.375 1.125-1.14 1.125h-1.196v-3.031c0-1.055-.125-1.54-.781-2.203Zm-.524-4.024V4.586l3.242 3.289h-2.86c-.265 0-.382-.11-.382-.383Zm-9.547 12.14V9.079c0-.719.375-1.125 1.133-1.125h2.399v4.281c0 1.118.554 1.664 1.664 1.664h4.125v5.735c0 .726-.375 1.125-1.133 1.125H6.539c-.758 0-1.133-.399-1.133-1.125Zm5.344-7.085c-.32 0-.46-.14-.46-.461V8.25l4.226 4.297H10.75Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></button></div><div data-pre-gradient="true"></div></div>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">Example with <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">getDefaultConfig</code>:</p>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1cc _1g1ptzo109 _1g1ptzo46 _1g1ptzo1yu" style="overflow:hidden"><pre class="hxfnim0 o4oa330"><code><div data-line="1" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">const config = getDefaultConfig({

</div></code></pre><div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1yk _1g1ptzo1zj _1g1ptzo23u" data-copy="true"><button class="hxfnim0 hxfnim9 _1ct8fpb1n _1g1ptzo5 _1g1ptzo2b4 _1g1ptzoe6 _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo2c0 _1g1ptzo2c2 _1g1ptzo3wu _1g1ptzo3x2 _1g1ptzo3x8 _1ct8fpb11 _1ct8fpb23 _1g1ptzo1ta _1g1ptzo1vd _1g1ptzol4 _1g1ptzomn _1ct8fpb7 _1g1ptzo3gd _1ct8fpbe _1g1ptzo230 _1g1ptzouf _1g1ptzo3w _1ct8fpb1m" tabindex="-1" style="background-color:var(--colors-lightBlue);box-shadow:0 0 8px var(--colors-fillElevated)"><svg fill="none" height="24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><title>Copy</title><path d="M3.875 19.727c0 1.687.867 2.562 2.54 2.562h7.312c1.671 0 2.53-.883 2.53-2.562V18.28h1.329c1.672 0 2.539-.875 2.539-2.562V9.53c0-1.023-.21-1.68-.828-2.312L15.398 3.25c-.585-.602-1.28-.828-2.18-.828h-2.945c-1.664 0-2.539.875-2.539 2.562v1.438h-1.32c-1.672 0-2.539.883-2.539 2.562v10.743Zm11.602-8.211L11.242 7.21c-.601-.61-1.11-.774-1.976-.781V5.07c0-.718.382-1.117 1.14-1.117h3.266v3.735c0 .968.515 1.468 1.476 1.468h3.446v6.469c0 .727-.375 1.125-1.14 1.125h-1.196v-3.031c0-1.055-.125-1.54-.781-2.203Zm-.524-4.024V4.586l3.242 3.289h-2.86c-.265 0-.382-.11-.382-.383Zm-9.547 12.14V9.079c0-.719.375-1.125 1.133-1.125h2.399v4.281c0 1.118.554 1.664 1.664 1.664h4.125v5.735c0 .726-.375 1.125-1.133 1.125H6.539c-.758 0-1.133-.399-1.133-1.125Zm5.344-7.085c-.32 0-.46-.14-.46-.461V8.25l4.226 4.297H10.75Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></button></div><div data-pre-gradient="true"></div></div>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">Example with <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">createConfig</code>:</p>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1cc _1g1ptzo109 _1g1ptzo46 _1g1ptzo1yu" style="overflow:hidden"><pre class="hxfnim0 o4oa330"><code><div data-line="1" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token inserted-sign inserted"><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line"> import { Chain } from &#x27;@rainbow-me/rainbowkit&#x27;</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line"> const chains: readonly [Chain, ...Chain[]] = [</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">   {</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">     ...mainnet,</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">     iconBackground: &#x27;#000&#x27;,</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">     iconUrl: &#x27;https://example.com/icons/ethereum.png&#x27;,</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">   },</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line"> ];</span>
<span class="token line"></span></span><span class="token unchanged"><span class="token prefix unchanged"> </span><span class="token line"> const config = createConfig({</span>

<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix unchanged"> </span><span class="token line">   transports: {</span>

<span class="token line"></span></span></div></code></pre><div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1yk _1g1ptzo1zj _1g1ptzo23u" data-copy="true"><button class="hxfnim0 hxfnim9 _1ct8fpb1n _1g1ptzo5 _1g1ptzo2b4 _1g1ptzoe6 _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo2c0 _1g1ptzo2c2 _1g1ptzo3wu _1g1ptzo3x2 _1g1ptzo3x8 _1ct8fpb11 _1ct8fpb23 _1g1ptzo1ta _1g1ptzo1vd _1g1ptzol4 _1g1ptzomn _1ct8fpb7 _1g1ptzo3gd _1ct8fpbe _1g1ptzo230 _1g1ptzouf _1g1ptzo3w _1ct8fpb1m" tabindex="-1" style="background-color:var(--colors-lightBlue);box-shadow:0 0 8px var(--colors-fillElevated)"><svg fill="none" height="24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><title>Copy</title><path d="M3.875 19.727c0 1.687.867 2.562 2.54 2.562h7.312c1.671 0 2.53-.883 2.53-2.562V18.28h1.329c1.672 0 2.539-.875 2.539-2.562V9.53c0-1.023-.21-1.68-.828-2.312L15.398 3.25c-.585-.602-1.28-.828-2.18-.828h-2.945c-1.664 0-2.539.875-2.539 2.562v1.438h-1.32c-1.672 0-2.539.883-2.539 2.562v10.743Zm11.602-8.211L11.242 7.21c-.601-.61-1.11-.774-1.976-.781V5.07c0-.718.382-1.117 1.14-1.117h3.266v3.735c0 .968.515 1.468 1.476 1.468h3.446v6.469c0 .727-.375 1.125-1.14 1.125h-1.196v-3.031c0-1.055-.125-1.54-.781-2.203Zm-.524-4.024V4.586l3.242 3.289h-2.86c-.265 0-.382-.11-.382-.383Zm-9.547 12.14V9.079c0-.719.375-1.125 1.133-1.125h2.399v4.281c0 1.118.554 1.664 1.664 1.664h4.125v5.735c0 .726-.375 1.125-1.133 1.125H6.539c-.758 0-1.133-.399-1.133-1.125Zm5.344-7.085c-.32 0-.46-.14-.46-.461V8.25l4.226 4.297H10.75Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></button></div><div data-pre-gradient="true"></div></div>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px"><strong>5. Custom Wallets</strong></p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">RainbowKit wallet connectors have undergone substantial changes to support Wagmi v2. Reference the <a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="https://www.rainbowkit.com/docs/custom-wallets">updated docs</a> and an <a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="https://github.com/rainbow-me/rainbowkit/blob/main/packages/rainbowkit/src/wallets/walletConnectors/rainbowWallet/rainbowWallet.ts">example connector</a> to upgrade any Custom Wallet Connectors in your dApp.</p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">Wallet connectors also now support the EIP-6963 standard with the <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">rdns</code> prop. Ensure that this is populated to prevent duplicate references to EIP-6963 supporting wallets in your wallet list.</p>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzozu _1g1ptzo1d6 _1g1ptzo2bo" id="1xx-breaking-changes"><a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="#1xx-breaking-changes"><h3 class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hd _1g1ptzoe1 _1g1ptzo2b6 fo5aobt _1g1ptzole fo5aobg fo5aobs">1.x.x Breaking changes</h3></a></div>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzozu _1g1ptzo1d1 _1g1ptzo2bo" id="updated-to-wagmi-v1"><a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="#updated-to-wagmi-v1"><h4 class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hd _1g1ptzoe1 _1g1ptzo2b6 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol9 fo5aobj fo5aobs">Updated to wagmi v1</h4></a></div>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">The <a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="https://wagmi.sh">wagmi</a> peer dependency has been updated to <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">1.x.x</code>.</p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">Follow the steps below to migrate.</p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px"><strong>1. Upgrade RainbowKit and <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">wagmi</code> to their latest version</strong></p>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1cc _1g1ptzo109 _1g1ptzo46 _1g1ptzo1yu" style="overflow:hidden"><pre class="hxfnim0 o4oa330"><code><div data-line="1" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token function">npm</span> i @rainbow-me/rainbowkit@^1 wagmi@^1

Install <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">viem</code> peer dependency</strong></p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">wagmi v1 requires the <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">viem</code> peer dependency. Install it with the following command:</p>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1cc _1g1ptzo109 _1g1ptzo46 _1g1ptzo1yu" style="overflow:hidden"><pre class="hxfnim0 o4oa330"><code><div data-line="1" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token function">npm</span> i viem
</div></code></pre><div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1yk _1g1ptzo1zj _1g1ptzo23u" data-copy="true"><button class="hxfnim0 hxfnim9 _1ct8fpb1n _1g1ptzo5 _1g1ptzo2b4 _1g1ptzoe6 _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo2c0 _1g1ptzo2c2 _1g1ptzo3wu _1g1ptzo3x2 _1g1ptzo3x8 _1ct8fpb11 _1ct8fpb23 _1g1ptzo1ta _1g1ptzo1vd _1g1ptzol4 _1g1ptzomn _1ct8fpb7 _1g1ptzo3gd _1ct8fpbe _1g1ptzo230 _1g1ptzouf _1g1ptzo3w _1ct8fpb1m" tabindex="-1" style="background-color:var(--colors-lightBlue);box-shadow:0 0 8px var(--colors-fillElevated)"><svg fill="none" height="24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><title>Copy</title><path d="M3.875 19.727c0 1.687.867 2.562 2.54 2.562h7.312c1.671 0 2.53-.883 2.53-2.562V18.28h1.329c1.672 0 2.539-.875 2.539-2.562V9.53c0-1.023-.21-1.68-.828-2.312L15.398 3.25c-.585-.602-1.28-.828-2.18-.828h-2.945c-1.664 0-2.539.875-2.539 2.562v1.438h-1.32c-1.672 0-2.539.883-2.539 2.562v10.743Zm11.602-8.211L11.242 7.21c-.601-.61-1.11-.774-1.976-.781V5.07c0-.718.382-1.117 1.14-1.117h3.266v3.735c0 .968.515 1.468 1.476 1.468h3.446v6.469c0 .727-.375 1.125-1.14 1.125h-1.196v-3.031c0-1.055-.125-1.54-.781-2.203Zm-.524-4.024V4.586l3.242 3.289h-2.86c-.265 0-.382-.11-.382-.383Zm-9.547 12.14V9.079c0-.719.375-1.125 1.133-1.125h2.399v4.281c0 1.118.554 1.664 1.664 1.664h4.125v5.735c0 .726-.375 1.125-1.133 1.125H6.539c-.758 0-1.133-.399-1.133-1.125Zm5.344-7.085c-.32 0-.46-.14-.46-.461V8.25l4.226 4.297H10.75Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></button></div><div data-pre-gradient="true"></div></div>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px"><strong>3. Ensure bundler and polyfill compatibility</strong></p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">Reference our <a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="https://github.com/rainbow-me/rainbowkit/blob/main/examples/with-next/next.config.js">Next.js Config</a> sample for configuration guidance for your project.</p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">Additional framework guides for Vite and Remix are available <a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="https://www.rainbowkit.com/docs/installation#additional-build-tooling-setup">here</a>.</p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px"><strong>4. Check for breaking changes in <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">wagmi</code></strong></p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">If you use <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">wagmi</code> hooks in your application, you will need to follow <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">wagmi</code>&#x27;s migration guide to v1.</p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px"><a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="https://wagmi.sh/react/migration-guide">You can see their migration guide here</a>.</p>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzozu _1g1ptzo1d6 _1g1ptzo2bo" id="012x-breaking-changes"><a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="#012x-breaking-changes"><h3 class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hd _1g1ptzoe1 _1g1ptzo2b6 fo5aobt _1g1ptzole fo5aobg fo5aobs">0.12.x Breaking changes</h3></a></div>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">The wagmi peer dependency has been updated to <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">0.12.x</code>.</p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">RainbowKit has adopted the <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">WalletConnectLegacyConnector</code> connector in <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">wagmi</code> for continued WalletConnect v1 support. Support for WalletConnect v2 and <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">WalletConnectConnector</code> will soon be available as a patch release, without breaking changes.</p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">Wallets will be transitioned automatically in future releases.</p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">Every dApp must now provide a <a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="https://cloud.walletconnect.com/">WalletConnect Cloud</a> <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">projectId</code> to enable WalletConnect v2. This must be completed before WalletConnect v1 bridge servers are shutdown on June 28, 2023. RainbowKit will quietly prefer v1 for all wallets if <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">projectId</code> is unspecified.</p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">Follow the steps below to migrate.</p>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzozu _1g1ptzo1d1 _1g1ptzo2bo" id="1-upgrade-rainbowkit-and-wagmi-to-their-latest-version"><a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="#1-upgrade-rainbowkit-and-wagmi-to-their-latest-version"><h4 class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hd _1g1ptzoe1 _1g1ptzo2b6 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol9 fo5aobj fo5aobs">1. Upgrade RainbowKit and <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">wagmi</code> to their latest version</h4></a></div>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1cc _1g1ptzo109 _1g1ptzo46 _1g1ptzo1yu" style="overflow:hidden"><pre class="hxfnim0 o4oa330"><code><div data-line="1" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token function">npm</span> i @rainbow-me/rainbowkit@^0.12.0 wagmi@^0.12.0
</div></code></pre><div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1yk _1g1ptzo1zj _1g1ptzo23u" data-copy="true"><button class="hxfnim0 hxfnim9 _1ct8fpb1n _1g1ptzo5 _1g1ptzo2b4 _1g1ptzoe6 _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo2c0 _1g1ptzo2c2 _1g1ptzo3wu _1g1ptzo3x2 _1g1ptzo3x8 _1ct8fpb11 _1ct8fpb23 _1g1ptzo1ta _1g1ptzo1vd _1g1ptzol4 _1g1ptzomn _1ct8fpb7 _1g1ptzo3gd _1ct8fpbe _1g1ptzo230 _1g1ptzouf _1g1ptzo3w _1ct8fpb1m" tabindex="-1" style="background-color:var(--colors-lightBlue);box-shadow:0 0 8px var(--colors-fillElevated)"><svg fill="none" height="24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><title>Copy</title><path d="M3.875 19.727c0 1.687.867 2.562 2.54 2.562h7.312c1.671 0 2.53-.883 2.53-2.562V18.28h1.329c1.672 0 2.539-.875 2.539-2.562V9.53c0-1.023-.21-1.68-.828-2.312L15.398 3.25c-.585-.602-1.28-.828-2.18-.828h-2.945c-1.664 0-2.539.875-2.539 2.562v1.438h-1.32c-1.672 0-2.539.883-2.539 2.562v10.743Zm11.602-8.211L11.242 7.21c-.601-.61-1.11-.774-1.976-.781V5.07c0-.718.382-1.117 1.14-1.117h3.266v3.735c0 .968.515 1.468 1.476 1.468h3.446v6.469c0 .727-.375 1.125-1.14 1.125h-1.196v-3.031c0-1.055-.125-1.54-.781-2.203Zm-.524-4.024V4.586l3.242 3.289h-2.86c-.265 0-.382-.11-.382-.383Zm-9.547 12.14V9.079c0-.719.375-1.125 1.133-1.125h2.399v4.281c0 1.118.554 1.664 1.664 1.664h4.125v5.735c0 .726-.375 1.125-1.133 1.125H6.539c-.758 0-1.133-.399-1.133-1.125Zm5.344-7.085c-.32 0-.46-.14-.46-.461V8.25l4.226 4.297H10.75Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></button></div><div data-pre-gradient="true"></div></div>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzozu _1g1ptzo1d1 _1g1ptzo2bo" id="2-supply-a-walletconnect-cloud-projectid"><a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="#2-supply-a-walletconnect-cloud-projectid"><h4 class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hd _1g1ptzoe1 _1g1ptzo2b6 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol9 fo5aobj fo5aobs">2. Supply a WalletConnect Cloud projectId</h4></a></div>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">Every dApp that relies on WalletConnect now needs to obtain a <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">projectId</code> from <a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="https://cloud.walletconnect.com/">WalletConnect Cloud</a>. This is absolutely free and only takes a few minutes.</p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">Provide the <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">projectId</code> to <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">getDefaultWallets</code> and individual RainbowKit wallet connectors like the following:</p>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1cc _1g1ptzo109 _1g1ptzo46 _1g1ptzo1yu" style="overflow:hidden"><pre class="hxfnim0 o4oa330"><code><div data-line="1" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token keyword">const</span> projectId <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">&#x27;YOUR_PROJECT_ID&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</div><div data-line="9" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token keyword">const</span> connectors <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">connectorsForWallets</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span>

<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">The wagmi peer dependency has been updated to <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">0.11.x</code>.</p>

<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">If you use <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">wagmi</code> hooks in your application, you will need to check if your application has been affected by the breaking changes in <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">wagmi</code>.</p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px"><a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="https://wagmi.sh/react/migration-guide#011x-breaking-changes">You can see their migration guide here</a>.</p>

<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzozu _1g1ptzo1d6 _1g1ptzo2bo" id="07x-breaking-changes"><a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="#07x-breaking-changes"><h3 class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hd _1g1ptzoe1 _1g1ptzo2b6 fo5aobt _1g1ptzole fo5aobg fo5aobs">0.7.x Breaking changes</h3></a></div>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">If you&#x27;re creating a custom wallet list, you must now import each wallet individually in order to reduce bundle size. Note that since wallets are no longer namespaced via the <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">wallet</code> object, all wallets now have a <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">Wallet</code> suffix.</p>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1cc _1g1ptzo109 _1g1ptzo46 _1g1ptzo1yu" style="overflow:hidden"><pre class="hxfnim0 o4oa330"><code><div data-line="1" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token deleted-sign deleted"><span class="token prefix deleted">-</span><span class="token line">import { connectorsForWallets, wallet } from &#x27;@rainbow-me/rainbowkit&#x27;;</span>
<span class="token line"></span></span><span class="token inserted-sign inserted"><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">import { connectorsForWallets } from &#x27;@rainbow-me/rainbowkit&#x27;;</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">import {</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">  injectedWallet,</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">  rainbowWallet,</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">  metaMaskWallet,</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">  coinbaseWallet,</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">  walletConnectWallet,</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">} from &#x27;@rainbow-me/rainbowkit/wallets&#x27;;</span>
<span class="token line"></span></span>
</div><div data-line="2" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">const wallets = [
</div><div data-line="3" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token deleted-sign deleted"><span class="token prefix deleted">-</span><span class="token line">  wallet.injected({ chains }),</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix deleted">-</span><span class="token line">  wallet.rainbow({ chains }),</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix deleted">-</span><span class="token line">  wallet.metaMask({ chains }),</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix deleted">-</span><span class="token line">  wallet.coinbase({ chains, appName: &#x27;My App&#x27; }),</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix deleted">-</span><span class="token line">  wallet.walletConnect({ chains }),</span>
<span class="token line"></span></span><span class="token inserted-sign inserted"><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">  injectedWallet({ chains }),</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">  rainbowWallet({ chains }),</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">  metaMaskWallet({ chains }),</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">  coinbaseWallet({ chains, appName: &#x27;My App&#x27; }),</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">  walletConnectWallet({ chains }),</span>
<span class="token line"></span></span>];
</div></code></pre><div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1yk _1g1ptzo1zj _1g1ptzo23u" data-copy="true"><button class="hxfnim0 hxfnim9 _1ct8fpb1n _1g1ptzo5 _1g1ptzo2b4 _1g1ptzoe6 _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo2c0 _1g1ptzo2c2 _1g1ptzo3wu _1g1ptzo3x2 _1g1ptzo3x8 _1ct8fpb11 _1ct8fpb23 _1g1ptzo1ta _1g1ptzo1vd _1g1ptzol4 _1g1ptzomn _1ct8fpb7 _1g1ptzo3gd _1ct8fpbe _1g1ptzo230 _1g1ptzouf _1g1ptzo3w _1ct8fpb1m" tabindex="-1" style="background-color:var(--colors-lightBlue);box-shadow:0 0 8px var(--colors-fillElevated)"><svg fill="none" height="24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><title>Copy</title><path d="M3.875 19.727c0 1.687.867 2.562 2.54 2.562h7.312c1.671 0 2.53-.883 2.53-2.562V18.28h1.329c1.672 0 2.539-.875 2.539-2.562V9.53c0-1.023-.21-1.68-.828-2.312L15.398 3.25c-.585-.602-1.28-.828-2.18-.828h-2.945c-1.664 0-2.539.875-2.539 2.562v1.438h-1.32c-1.672 0-2.539.883-2.539 2.562v10.743Zm11.602-8.211L11.242 7.21c-.601-.61-1.11-.774-1.976-.781V5.07c0-.718.382-1.117 1.14-1.117h3.266v3.735c0 .968.515 1.468 1.476 1.468h3.446v6.469c0 .727-.375 1.125-1.14 1.125h-1.196v-3.031c0-1.055-.125-1.54-.781-2.203Zm-.524-4.024V4.586l3.242 3.289h-2.86c-.265 0-.382-.11-.382-.383Zm-9.547 12.14V9.079c0-.719.375-1.125 1.133-1.125h2.399v4.281c0 1.118.554 1.664 1.664 1.664h4.125v5.735c0 .726-.375 1.125-1.133 1.125H6.539c-.758 0-1.133-.399-1.133-1.125Zm5.344-7.085c-.32 0-.46-.14-.46-.461V8.25l4.226 4.297H10.75Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></button></div><div data-pre-gradient="true"></div></div>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">Also note that the Steakwallet backwards compatibility layer has been removed. Omni should be used instead.</p>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1cc _1g1ptzo109 _1g1ptzo46 _1g1ptzo1yu" style="overflow:hidden"><pre class="hxfnim0 o4oa330"><code><div data-line="1" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token deleted-sign deleted"><span class="token prefix deleted">-</span><span class="token line">import { wallet } from &#x27;@rainbow-me/rainbowkit&#x27;;</span>
<span class="token line"></span></span><span class="token inserted-sign inserted"><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">import { omniWallet } from &#x27;@rainbow-me/rainbowkit/wallets&#x27;;</span>
<span class="token line"></span></span>
</div><div data-line="2" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">const wallets = [
</div><div data-line="3" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token deleted-sign deleted"><span class="token prefix deleted">-</span><span class="token line">  wallet.steak({ chains }),</span>
<span class="token line"></span></span><span class="token inserted-sign inserted"><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">  omniWallet({ chains }),</span>
<span class="token line"></span></span>];
</div></code></pre><div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1yk _1g1ptzo1zj _1g1ptzo23u" data-copy="true"><button class="hxfnim0 hxfnim9 _1ct8fpb1n _1g1ptzo5 _1g1ptzo2b4 _1g1ptzoe6 _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo2c0 _1g1ptzo2c2 _1g1ptzo3wu _1g1ptzo3x2 _1g1ptzo3x8 _1ct8fpb11 _1ct8fpb23 _1g1ptzo1ta _1g1ptzo1vd _1g1ptzol4 _1g1ptzomn _1ct8fpb7 _1g1ptzo3gd _1ct8fpbe _1g1ptzo230 _1g1ptzouf _1g1ptzo3w _1ct8fpb1m" tabindex="-1" style="background-color:var(--colors-lightBlue);box-shadow:0 0 8px var(--colors-fillElevated)"><svg fill="none" height="24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><title>Copy</title><path d="M3.875 19.727c0 1.687.867 2.562 2.54 2.562h7.312c1.671 0 2.53-.883 2.53-2.562V18.28h1.329c1.672 0 2.539-.875 2.539-2.562V9.53c0-1.023-.21-1.68-.828-2.312L15.398 3.25c-.585-.602-1.28-.828-2.18-.828h-2.945c-1.664 0-2.539.875-2.539 2.562v1.438h-1.32c-1.672 0-2.539.883-2.539 2.562v10.743Zm11.602-8.211L11.242 7.21c-.601-.61-1.11-.774-1.976-.781V5.07c0-.718.382-1.117 1.14-1.117h3.266v3.735c0 .968.515 1.468 1.476 1.468h3.446v6.469c0 .727-.375 1.125-1.14 1.125h-1.196v-3.031c0-1.055-.125-1.54-.781-2.203Zm-.524-4.024V4.586l3.242 3.289h-2.86c-.265 0-.382-.11-.382-.383Zm-9.547 12.14V9.079c0-.719.375-1.125 1.133-1.125h2.399v4.281c0 1.118.554 1.664 1.664 1.664h4.125v5.735c0 .726-.375 1.125-1.133 1.125H6.539c-.758 0-1.133-.399-1.133-1.125Zm5.344-7.085c-.32 0-.46-.14-.46-.461V8.25l4.226 4.297H10.75Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></button></div><div data-pre-gradient="true"></div></div>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzozu _1g1ptzo1d6 _1g1ptzo2bo" id="04x-breaking-changes"><a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="#04x-breaking-changes"><h3 class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hd _1g1ptzoe1 _1g1ptzo2b6 fo5aobt _1g1ptzole fo5aobg fo5aobs">0.4.x Breaking changes</h3></a></div>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">RainbowKit has updated the <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">wagmi</code> peer dependency to <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">0.5.x</code>.</p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">Follow the steps below to migrate.</p>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzozu _1g1ptzo1d1 _1g1ptzo2bo" id="1-upgrade-dependencies"><a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="#1-upgrade-dependencies"><h4 class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hd _1g1ptzoe1 _1g1ptzo2b6 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol9 fo5aobj fo5aobs">1. Upgrade dependencies</h4></a></div>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">Upgrade RainbowKit and wagmi to their latest version</p>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1cc _1g1ptzo109 _1g1ptzo46 _1g1ptzo1yu" style="overflow:hidden"><pre class="hxfnim0 o4oa330"><code><div data-line="1" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token function">npm</span> i @rainbow-me/rainbowkit@^0.4.0 wagmi@^0.5.0
</div></code></pre><div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1yk _1g1ptzo1zj _1g1ptzo23u" data-copy="true"><button class="hxfnim0 hxfnim9 _1ct8fpb1n _1g1ptzo5 _1g1ptzo2b4 _1g1ptzoe6 _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo2c0 _1g1ptzo2c2 _1g1ptzo3wu _1g1ptzo3x2 _1g1ptzo3x8 _1ct8fpb11 _1ct8fpb23 _1g1ptzo1ta _1g1ptzo1vd _1g1ptzol4 _1g1ptzomn _1ct8fpb7 _1g1ptzo3gd _1ct8fpbe _1g1ptzo230 _1g1ptzouf _1g1ptzo3w _1ct8fpb1m" tabindex="-1" style="background-color:var(--colors-lightBlue);box-shadow:0 0 8px var(--colors-fillElevated)"><svg fill="none" height="24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><title>Copy</title><path d="M3.875 19.727c0 1.687.867 2.562 2.54 2.562h7.312c1.671 0 2.53-.883 2.53-2.562V18.28h1.329c1.672 0 2.539-.875 2.539-2.562V9.53c0-1.023-.21-1.68-.828-2.312L15.398 3.25c-.585-.602-1.28-.828-2.18-.828h-2.945c-1.664 0-2.539.875-2.539 2.562v1.438h-1.32c-1.672 0-2.539.883-2.539 2.562v10.743Zm11.602-8.211L11.242 7.21c-.601-.61-1.11-.774-1.976-.781V5.07c0-.718.382-1.117 1.14-1.117h3.266v3.735c0 .968.515 1.468 1.476 1.468h3.446v6.469c0 .727-.375 1.125-1.14 1.125h-1.196v-3.031c0-1.055-.125-1.54-.781-2.203Zm-.524-4.024V4.586l3.242 3.289h-2.86c-.265 0-.382-.11-.382-.383Zm-9.547 12.14V9.079c0-.719.375-1.125 1.133-1.125h2.399v4.281c0 1.118.554 1.664 1.664 1.664h4.125v5.735c0 .726-.375 1.125-1.133 1.125H6.539c-.758 0-1.133-.399-1.133-1.125Zm5.344-7.085c-.32 0-.46-.14-.46-.461V8.25l4.226 4.297H10.75Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></button></div><div data-pre-gradient="true"></div></div>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzozu _1g1ptzo1d1 _1g1ptzo2bo" id="2-check-for-breaking-changes-in-wagmi-4"><a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="#2-check-for-breaking-changes-in-wagmi-4"><h4 class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hd _1g1ptzoe1 _1g1ptzo2b6 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol9 fo5aobj fo5aobs">2. Check for breaking changes in <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">wagmi</code></h4></a></div>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">If you use <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">wagmi</code> hooks in your application, you will need to check if your application has been affected by the breaking changes in <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">wagmi</code>.</p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px"><a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="https://wagmi.sh/react/migration-guide#05x-breaking-changes">You can see their migration guide here</a>.</p>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzozu _1g1ptzo1d6 _1g1ptzo2bo" id="03x-breaking-changes"><a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="#03x-breaking-changes"><h3 class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hd _1g1ptzoe1 _1g1ptzo2b6 fo5aobt _1g1ptzole fo5aobg fo5aobs">0.3.x Breaking changes</h3></a></div>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">Removed the <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">chainId</code> parameter from <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">createConnector</code> on the <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">Wallet</code> type.</p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px"><strong>Note that all built-in wallets are using the new API. Most consumers will be unaffected. This change only affects consumers that have created/consumed <a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="/docs/custom-wallets">custom wallets</a>.</strong></p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">If you previously derived RPC URLs from the <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">chainId</code> on <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">createConnector</code>, you can now remove that logic as <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">wagmi</code> now handles RPC URLs internally when used with <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">configureChains</code>.</p>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1cc _1g1ptzo109 _1g1ptzo46 _1g1ptzo1yu" style="overflow:hidden"><pre class="hxfnim0 o4oa330"><code><div data-line="1" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">import { connectorsForWallets, wallet, Chain, Wallet } from &#x27;@rainbow-me/rainbowkit&#x27;;
</div><div data-line="2" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">import { chain, configureChains } from &#x27;wagmi&#x27;;
</div><div data-line="3" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">import { alchemyProvider } from &#x27;wagmi/providers/alchemy&#x27;;
</div><div data-line="4" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">import { publicProvider } from &#x27;wagmi/providers/public&#x27;;
</div><div data-line="5" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">import { WalletConnectConnector } from &#x27;wagmi/connectors/walletConnect&#x27;;
</div><div data-line="6" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">
</div><div data-line="7" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">export interface MyWalletOptions {
</div><div data-line="8" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token unchanged"><span class="token prefix unchanged"> </span><span class="token line"> chains: Chain[];</span>
<span class="token line"></span></span>}
</div><div data-line="9" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">
</div><div data-line="10" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token deleted-sign deleted"><span class="token prefix deleted">-</span><span class="token line">const chains = [chain.mainnet]</span>
<span class="token line"></span></span><span class="token inserted-sign inserted"><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">const { chains } = configureChains(</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">  [chain.mainnet],</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">  [</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">    alchemyProvider({ alchemyId: process.env.ALCHEMY_ID }),</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">    publicProvider(),</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">  ]</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line">);</span>
<span class="token line"></span></span>
</div><div data-line="11" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">export const rainbow = ({ chains }: MyWalletOptions): Wallet =&gt; ({
</div><div data-line="12" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token unchanged"><span class="token prefix unchanged"> </span><span class="token line"> ...</span>
<span class="token line"></span></span><span class="token deleted-sign deleted"><span class="token prefix deleted">-</span><span class="token line"> createConnector: ({ chainId }) =&gt; {</span>
<span class="token line"></span></span><span class="token inserted-sign inserted"><span class="token prefix inserted">+</span><span class="token line"> createConnector: () =&gt; {</span>
<span class="token line"></span></span><span class="token deleted-sign deleted"><span class="token prefix deleted">-</span><span class="token line">   const rpc = chains.reduce(</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix deleted">-</span><span class="token line">     (rpcUrlMap, chain) =&gt; ({</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix deleted">-</span><span class="token line">       ...rpcUrlMap,</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix deleted">-</span><span class="token line">       [chainId]: chain.rpcUrls.default,</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix deleted">-</span><span class="token line">     }),</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix deleted">-</span><span class="token line">     {}</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix deleted">-</span><span class="token line">   );</span>
<span class="token line"></span></span><span class="token unchanged"><span class="token prefix unchanged"> </span><span class="token line">   const connector = new WalletConnectConnector({</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix unchanged"> </span><span class="token line">     chains,</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix unchanged"> </span><span class="token line">     options: {</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix unchanged"> </span><span class="token line">       qrcode: false,</span>
<span class="token line"></span></span><span class="token deleted-sign deleted"><span class="token prefix deleted">-</span><span class="token line">       rpc,</span>
<span class="token line"></span></span><span class="token unchanged"><span class="token prefix unchanged"> </span><span class="token line">     },</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix unchanged"> </span><span class="token line">   });</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix unchanged"> </span><span class="token line"> }</span>
<span class="token line"></span><span class="token prefix unchanged"> </span><span class="token line"> ...</span>
<span class="token line"></span></span>}
</div><div data-line="13" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">
</div><div data-line="14" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true">const connectors = connectorsForWallets([

</div></code></pre><div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1yk _1g1ptzo1zj _1g1ptzo23u" data-copy="true"><button class="hxfnim0 hxfnim9 _1ct8fpb1n _1g1ptzo5 _1g1ptzo2b4 _1g1ptzoe6 _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo2c0 _1g1ptzo2c2 _1g1ptzo3wu _1g1ptzo3x2 _1g1ptzo3x8 _1ct8fpb11 _1ct8fpb23 _1g1ptzo1ta _1g1ptzo1vd _1g1ptzol4 _1g1ptzomn _1ct8fpb7 _1g1ptzo3gd _1ct8fpbe _1g1ptzo230 _1g1ptzouf _1g1ptzo3w _1ct8fpb1m" tabindex="-1" style="background-color:var(--colors-lightBlue);box-shadow:0 0 8px var(--colors-fillElevated)"><svg fill="none" height="24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><title>Copy</title><path d="M3.875 19.727c0 1.687.867 2.562 2.54 2.562h7.312c1.671 0 2.53-.883 2.53-2.562V18.28h1.329c1.672 0 2.539-.875 2.539-2.562V9.53c0-1.023-.21-1.68-.828-2.312L15.398 3.25c-.585-.602-1.28-.828-2.18-.828h-2.945c-1.664 0-2.539.875-2.539 2.562v1.438h-1.32c-1.672 0-2.539.883-2.539 2.562v10.743Zm11.602-8.211L11.242 7.21c-.601-.61-1.11-.774-1.976-.781V5.07c0-.718.382-1.117 1.14-1.117h3.266v3.735c0 .968.515 1.468 1.476 1.468h3.446v6.469c0 .727-.375 1.125-1.14 1.125h-1.196v-3.031c0-1.055-.125-1.54-.781-2.203Zm-.524-4.024V4.586l3.242 3.289h-2.86c-.265 0-.382-.11-.382-.383Zm-9.547 12.14V9.079c0-.719.375-1.125 1.133-1.125h2.399v4.281c0 1.118.554 1.664 1.664 1.664h4.125v5.735c0 .726-.375 1.125-1.133 1.125H6.539c-.758 0-1.133-.399-1.133-1.125Zm5.344-7.085c-.32 0-.46-.14-.46-.461V8.25l4.226 4.297H10.75Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></button></div><div data-pre-gradient="true"></div></div>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzozu _1g1ptzo1d6 _1g1ptzo2bo" id="02x-breaking-changes"><a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="#02x-breaking-changes"><h3 class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hd _1g1ptzoe1 _1g1ptzo2b6 fo5aobt _1g1ptzole fo5aobg fo5aobs">0.2.x Breaking changes</h3></a></div>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">RainbowKit has updated the <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">wagmi</code> peer dependency to <code class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1sl _1g1ptzo1uo _1g1ptzo2q9 _1g1ptzo3m _1g1ptzo2b7 _1g1ptzokz _1g1ptzo1s1 _1g1ptzo2c9 _1nh4n351 _1g1ptzo3gp">^0.4</code>.</p>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">Follow the steps below to migrate.</p>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzozu _1g1ptzo1d1 _1g1ptzo2bo" id="1-upgrade-dependencies-1"><a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="#1-upgrade-dependencies-1"><h4 class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hd _1g1ptzoe1 _1g1ptzo2b6 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol9 fo5aobj fo5aobs">1. Upgrade dependencies</h4></a></div>
<p class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hh _1g1ptzo2b6 _1g1ptzo109 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol4 fo5aob1 fo5aobr" style="font-weight:500;line-height:25px">Upgrade RainbowKit and wagmi to their latest version</p>
<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo1cc _1g1ptzo109 _1g1ptzo46 _1g1ptzo1yu" style="overflow:hidden"><pre class="hxfnim0 o4oa330"><code><div data-line="1" class="highlight-line" data-highlighted="true"><span class="token function">npm</span> i @rainbow-me/rainbowkit@^0.2.0 wagmi@^0.4.2

<div class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzozu _1g1ptzo1d1 _1g1ptzo2bo" id="2-replace-configurechains-import"><a class="hxfnim0 hxfnima _1e8lv5k3 _1e8lv5k0 _1g1ptzo3gd _1g1ptzo3hf" href="#2-replace-configurechains-import"><h4 class="hxfnim0 _1g1ptzo3hd _1g1ptzoe1 _1g1ptzo2b6 fo5aobt _1g1ptzol9 fo5aobj fo5aobs">2.
